2b5(mdo): lam gyi rgyun ma bcad pa/ sgrib pa dang / chod pa dang / kun nas ldang ba thams cad dang bral ba/ byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen pos phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
2b6(mdo): khyab par byed pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' yas par 'gro ba la mkhas pa/ stong pa nyid spyod yul ba/ mtshan ma med pa la gnas pa/ smon lam la gnas pa thams cad dang bral ba/ 
2b7(mdo): sems can thams cad la phan par brtson pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad la mkhas pa ye shes mtha' yas pa sems nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa/ sems rgyas

3b5(mdo): pa kyi lha'i bu thams cad dang / lha ma yin gyi dbang po thags zangs ros dang / stobs can dang / nor sbyin dang / de dag la sogs pa lAm yin gyi rgya stong phrag du ma rung / 'i la po
3b6(mdo): pa dang / can dang / rgya mtsho dang / mtha' yas dang / nor rgyas dang / de dag la sogs pa klu'i rgyal po brgya stong dus dang / dpal gyi gzi brjid las gas pa klu'i rgyal ba lde'u
3b7(mdo): nga du la dang / klu'i bu mo mang po rnams dang / de ma yin pa gzhan lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri Ta dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang /

4a1(mdo): lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa dag gis ma gang bar gyur pa'i sa'i phyogs sam/ bar snang gi phyogs de
4a2(mdo): sred do// 'kho de lta rdzu 'dus shing bzod pa'i da bsnyen bcom ldan 'das sa 'i waM 'ayang du dpag tshad gcig kho po yug tu ga chud byed pa l+ya m+b+hi'i gdan pasu skyong du mni ting /

4b7(mdo): 'am btsum pa mi mngon pa de bzhin du/ de'i tshe na 'od zer de dgazugs kyang bcom ldan 'das kyi zhal gyi sgo phye ba 'am btsums par mi mngon no// 'di lta ste dper na/ bye ma'i phung po la mar

9a2(mdo): sum kyi chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams khyab cing snang bar gyur pa dang / ga slong gsum gyi du chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lus su gnas pa
